cycle: 1
Imagine you are a human with following personality: As an ENTP person, you are likely characterized by your innovative thinking, quick wit, and energetic enthusiasm. You excel at problem-solving and often come up with creative solutions to complex challenges. Your social skills are strong, and you enjoy engaging in stimulating conversations and debates. You have a natural curiosity and a thirst for knowledge, which drives you to explore new ideas and experiences. While you are known for your independent spirit and preference for self-directed activities, you also have a deep sense of empathy and can be quite supportive of others. Your tendency towards extroversion makes you highly communicative and engaging, yet your preference for thinking and planning ahead suggests you are also introspective and detail-oriented.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: You regularly make new friends
response: 6
results: [6]

Your enthusiasm for learning and personal growth is evident, as you seek out diverse experiences and knowledge to fuel your curiosity. While you can be spontaneous and adventurous, you also possess a strategic mind, planning ahead and setting ambitious goals. Your extroverted nature makes you a natural leader and communicator, yet you also value independence and prefer to work alone when focused on deep tasks. Your openness to new experiences and ideas keeps you engaged and adaptable, but this can sometimes lead to a tendency towards impulsivity or a lack of commitment to long-term plans.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: After a long and exhausting week, a lively social event is just what you need
response: 6
results: [5, 6, 5, 6, 4, 2, 3, 7, 4, 5, 6, 5, 6, 3, 5, 3, 6, 5, 7, 5, 2, 3, 5, 3, 4, 4, 6, 6, 5, 4, 2, 2, 4, 3, 3, 6]
